The area replaced "[A Bug's Land](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Bug%27s_Land "A Bug's Land")", which closed in mid-2018 to begin construction of the Marvel area.[[376]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-VarietyDisneyParks-380)[[384]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-DisneyParksMar2018-388)[Tom Holland](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tom_Holland "Tom Holland") reprises his role as [Peter Parker / Spider-Man](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peter_Parker_(Marvel_Cinematic_Universe) "Peter Parker (Marvel Cinematic Universe)") in the attraction [Web Slingers: A Spider-Man Adventure](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Web_Slingers:_A_Spider-Man_Adventure "Web Slingers: A Spider-Man Adventure"), in which Parker has set up W.E.B. (the Worldwide Engineers Brigade) to inspire a new generation to use technology to save the world. Riders are recruited by Spider-Man into the initiative to stop his malfunctioning Spider-Bots.[[391]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-HollandWebSlingers-395) Web Slingers was directed by _Spider-Man_ director Jon Watts along with Brett Strong, and was written by Steven Spiegel and featured visual effects by [Framestore](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Framestore "Framestore").[[392]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-WaittWebSlingers-396) A one-act version of _[Rogers: The Musical](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rogers:\_The\_Musical "Rogers: The Musical")_ premiered at the [Hyperion Theater](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hyperion_Theater "Hyperion Theater") on June 30, 2023, and ran for a limited time until August 31.[[393]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-RogersMusicalDCA-397)

#### Walt Disney Studios Park

In March 2018, the Walt Disney Company announced a new Marvel-themed area inspired by the MCU to [Disneyland Paris](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Disneyland_Paris "Disneyland Paris")' Walt Disney Studios Park. The area includes a reimagined attraction where riders team up with Iron Man and other Avengers on a "hyper-kinetic adventure" on July 20, 2022.[[376]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-VarietyDisneyParks-380)[[394]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-DisneyParisJuly2022-398) The park also hosted the "Summer of Super Heroes" live-action stage show from June–September 2018.[[376]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-VarietyDisneyParks-380)[[384]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-DisneyParksMar2018-388)

### Disney cruises

Main articles: [Disney Wish](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Disney_Wish "Disney Wish") and [Disney Treasure](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Disney_Treasure "Disney Treasure")

In July 2021, the immersive family dining experience "**Avengers: Quantum Encounter**" at the Worlds of Marvel restaurant on the _Disney Wish_ cruise ship was announced, which debuted when the cruise began voyages on July 14, 2022.[[395]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-DisneyWish-399)[[396]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-DisneyWishDelay-400) The experience takes place during dinner with interactive elements and a full CGI recreation of the _Wish_'s upper decks.[[397]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-QuantumEncounterPolygon-401)[Paul Rudd](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paul_Rudd "Paul Rudd"), [Evangeline Lilly](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Evangeline_Lilly "Evangeline Lilly"), [Anthony Mackie](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anthony_Mackie "Anthony Mackie"), [Brie Larson](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brie_Larson "Brie Larson"), [Kerry Condon](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kerry_Condon "Kerry Condon"), and [Iman Vellani](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iman_Vellani "Iman Vellani") reprised their MCU roles,[[398]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-QuantumEncounter-402)[[399]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-VellaniQuantumEncounter-403) while [Ross Marquand](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ross_Marquand "Ross Marquand") voiced [Ultron](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ultron_(Marvel_Cinematic_Universe) "Ultron (Marvel Cinematic Universe)") after previously doing so in _[What If...?](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/What\_If...%3F\_(TV\_series) "What If...? (TV series)")_, in which he replaced [James Spader](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Spader "James Spader").[[398]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-QuantumEncounter-402)[Chris Waitt](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chris_Waitt "Chris Waitt") directed Rudd and Lilly's content, which was written by Steven Spiegel and featured visual effects by Framestore.[[400]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-WaittQuantumEncounter-404)[[401]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-WaittWebsite-405)_The Marvels_ director [Nia DaCosta](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nia_DaCosta "Nia DaCosta") filmed Vellani and Larson's content in London ahead of principal photography for the film.[[402]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-DaCostaQuantumEncounter-406)

In September 2023, the _Wish_'s [sister ship](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sister_ship "Sister ship") the _[Disney Treasure](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Disney\_Treasure "Disney Treasure")_ was announced to also include the Worlds of Marvel restaurant with two nights of distinct shows and menus, featuring an appearance by Spider-Man. The Marvel Super Hero Academy is also included on the cruise, where young kids can train to be superheroes with Spider-Man, Black Panther, and Ant-Man. These were available on the _Treasure_ when it began voyages on December 21, 2024.[[403]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-DisneyTreasure-407)

### Other live attractions

#### _Avengers S.T.A.T.I.O.N._

In May 2014, the _Avengers S.T.A.T.I.O.N._ (Scientific Training and Tactical Intelligence Operative Network) exhibit opened at the [Discovery Times Square](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Discovery_Times_Square "Discovery Times Square") center. The exhibit features replica set pieces and props from the films, mixed with interactive technology and information, crafted through a partnership with [NASA](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/NASA "NASA") and other scientists. [Titus Welliver](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Titus_Welliver "Titus Welliver") also provides a "debrief" to visitors, reprising his role as S.H.I.E.L.D. agent [Felix Blake](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Felix_Blake "Felix Blake"). Created by Victory Hill Exhibits, _Avengers S.T.A.T.I.O.N._ cost $7.5 million to create,[[404]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-AvengersSTATIONDailyNews-408)[[405]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-AvengersSTATIONEW-409) and ran through early September 2015.[[406]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-AvengersSTATIONClosing-410)

The exhibit also opened in [South Korea](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/South_Korea "South Korea") at the [War Memorial of Korea](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/War_Memorial_of_Korea "War Memorial of Korea") in April 2015,[[407]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-STATIONKorea-411)[[408]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-STATIONLasVegas-412) in Paris, France, at [Esplanade de La Défense](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Esplanade_de_La_D%C3%A9fense_(Paris_M%C3%A9tro) "Esplanade de La Défense (Paris Métro)") a year later, and in Las Vegas at the [Treasure Island Hotel and Casino](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Treasure_Island_Hotel_and_Casino "Treasure Island Hotel and Casino") in June 2016.[[408]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-STATIONLasVegas-412) The Las Vegas version of the exhibit featured updated character details and corresponding science to incorporate the Marvel films that were released since the original exhibit in New York. Additionally, the Las Vegas version features Cobie Smulders reprising her role as Maria Hill to "debrief" visitors, replacing Welliver.[[409]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-STATIONLasVegas2-413)

#### GOMA exhibit

An art exhibit, titled _Marvel: Creating the Cinematic Universe_, was displayed exclusively at the [Queensland Gallery of Modern Art](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Queensland_Gallery_of_Modern_Art "Queensland Gallery of Modern Art") (GOMA) in Brisbane, Australia, in 2017. The exhibit, which included "300 plus objects, films, costumes, drawings and other ephemera", featured content "from the collection of Marvel Studios and Marvel Entertainment and private collections" with "significant focus [given] to the creative artists who translate the drawn narrative to the screen through production design and storyboarding, costume and prop design, and special effects and post-production". _Marvel: Creating the Cinematic Universe_ was also extended to GOMA's Australian Cinémathèque with a retrospective of the MCU films.[[410]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-GOMA-414)[[411]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-GOMASMH-415)

#### _Avengers: Damage Control_

In October 2019, Marvel Studios and [ILMxLAB](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ILMxLAB "ILMxLAB") announced the [virtual reality](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_reality "Virtual reality") experience _Avengers: Damage Control_. The experience was available for a limited time starting in mid-October 2019 at select [Void VR](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Void_(virtual_reality) "The Void (virtual reality)") locations. _Avengers: Damage Control_ sees players taking control of one of Shuri's Emergency Response Suits–which combine Wakandan and Stark Industries technologies–to defeat a threat alongside Doctor Strange, Ant-Man, and the Wasp. [Letitia Wright](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Letitia_Wright "Letitia Wright"), [Benedict Cumberbatch](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Benedict_Cumberbatch "Benedict Cumberbatch"), [Paul Rudd](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paul_Rudd "Paul Rudd"), and [Evangeline Lilly](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Evangeline_Lilly "Evangeline Lilly") all reprise their MCU roles,[[412]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-VRDamageControl-416) while Ross Marquand voices Ultron, replacing James Spader.[[413]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MarquandDC-417) The experience was extended to the end of 2019.[[414]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-VRDamageControlExtended-418)

### Marvel Studios' Infinity Saga Concert Experience

In May 2024, the Marvel Studios' Infinity Saga Concert Experience was announced by Disney Concerts, Marvel Studios, and the [Los Angeles Philharmonic](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Los_Angeles_Philharmonic "Los Angeles Philharmonic"), to premiere on August 30 and 31, 2024, at the [Hollywood Bowl](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hollywood_Bowl "Hollywood Bowl"). The concert, conducted by the Philharmonic's Music and Artistic director [Gustavo Dudamel](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gustavo_Dudamel "Gustavo Dudamel"), features the Philharmonic performing a "specially created score" of music from the Infinity Saga films, such as _The Avengers_ theme and "[Portals](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avengers_assemble_scene#Music "Avengers assemble scene")" from _Avengers: Endgame_, live to picture.[[415]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-ConcertExperience-419) The first half of the concert focused on individual characters from the films, while the second half centered on _Avengers: Infinity War_ and _Avengers: Endgame_. A "post-credits scene" saw the Philharmonic play [Michael Giacchino](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Giacchino "Michael Giacchino")'s theme from _[The Fantastic Four: First Steps](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The\_Fantastic\_Four:\_First\_Steps "The Fantastic Four: First Steps")_ (2025).[[416]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-ConcertExperienceTour-420) The performance also used [projection mapping](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Projection_mapping "Projection mapping") on the proscenium of the Hollywood Bowl while audiences members wore [PixMob](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/PixMob "PixMob") light-up wrist bands.[[415]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-ConcertExperience-419)[[417]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-ConcertExperienceTour2-421) The concert is set to go on tour globally in 2025.[[416]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-ConcertExperienceTour-420)[[417]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-ConcertExperienceTour2-421)

### Live-action specials

#### _Marvel Studios: Assembling a Universe_ (2014)

On March 18, 2014, ABC aired a one-hour [television special](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Television_special "Television special") titled _Marvel Studios: Assembling a Universe_, which documented the history of Marvel Studios and the development of the Marvel Cinematic Universe and included exclusive interviews and behind-the-scenes footage from all of the films, One-Shots, and _Agents of S.H.I.E.L.D._, and sneak peeks of _Avengers: Age of Ultron_, _Captain America: The Winter Soldier_, _Guardians of the Galaxy_, unaired episodes of _Agents of S.H.I.E.L.D._,[[418]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-TVSpecial-422) and _Ant-Man_.[[419]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-TVSpecialAntMan-423) Brian Lowry of _Variety_ felt the special, "contains a pretty interesting business and creative story. While it might all make sense in hindsight, there was appreciable audacity in Marvel's plan to release five loosely connected movies from the same hero-filled world, beginning with the cinematically unproven _Iron Man_ and culminating with superhero team _The Avengers_. As such, this fast-moving hour qualifies as more than just a cut-and-paste job from electronic press kits, although there's an element of that, certainly."[[420]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-VarietySpecialReview-424) The special was released on September 9, 2014, on the home media for _Agents of S.H.I.E.L.D._ season 1.[[421]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-SHIELDS1HomeMedia-425)

#### _Marvel 75 Years: From Pulp to Pop!_ (2014)

In September 2014, _Agents of S.H.I.E.L.D._ executive producer Jeffrey Bell stated that to meet production demands and avoid having to air repeat episodes, ABC would likely air a Marvel special in place of a regular installment at some point during the first ten episodes of _Agents of S.H.I.E.L.D._'s second season.[[422]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-BellSep2014-426) In October, the special was revealed to be _Marvel 75 Years: From Pulp to Pop!_, which was hosted by [Emily VanCamp](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emily_VanCamp "Emily VanCamp"), who portrays [Agent 13](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sharon_Carter_(Marvel_Cinematic_Universe) "Sharon Carter (Marvel Cinematic Universe)") in _Captain America: The Winter Soldier_, and aired on November 4, 2014.[[423]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-PulptoPop-427) The special features behind the scenes footage from _Avengers: Age of Ultron_ and _Ant-Man_, as well as footage from the _Agent Carter_ television series previously screened at [New York Comic Con](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_York_Comic_Con "New York Comic Con").[[424]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-IGNSpecial2Review-428) Brian Lowry of _Variety_ felt an hour for the special did not "do the topic justice" adding, "For anyone who has seen more than one Marvel movie but would shrug perplexedly at the mention of Jack Kirby or [Steve Ditko](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Steve_Ditko "Steve Ditko"), _Marvel 75 Years: From Pulp To Pop!_ should probably be required viewing. Fun, fast-paced and encompassing many of the company's highlights along with a few lowlights, it's a solid primer on Marvel's history, while weaving in inevitable self-promotion and synergistic plugs."[[425]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-VarietySpecial2Review-429) Eric Goldman of IGN also wished the special had been longer, adding, "Understandably, the more you already know about Marvel, the less you'll be surprised by _Marvel 75 Years: From Pulp to Pop!_, but it's important to remember who this special is really made for – a mainstream audience who have embraced the Marvel characters, via the hugely successful movies, in a way no one could have imagined."[[424]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-IGNSpecial2Review-428)

#### _Marvel Studios: Expanding the Universe_ (2019)

The special _Expanding the Universe_ was released on Disney+ on November 12, 2019. It features a look at the original MCU TV series for Disney+, with interviews and concept art.[[426]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-ExpandingTheUniverse-430)

#### Bilibili New Year's Gala (2020)

A Marvel-themed orchestra performance of an extended version of [Brian Tyler](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brian_Tyler "Brian Tyler")'s Marvel Studios theme and [Alan Silvestri](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alan_Silvestri "Alan Silvestri")'s theme from _The Avengers_ took place during China's Bilibili New Year's Gala on December 31, 2020, to promote the 2021 Marvel Studios film releases.[[427]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-BilibiliPerformance-431)[[428]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-BilibiliPerformance2-432)

#### _Marvel Studios' 2021 Disney+ Day Special_ (2021)

A special titled _Marvel Studios' 2021 Disney+ Day Special_, which looked at the future of the MCU on Disney+, was released on the service on November 12, 2021, as part of its "[Disney+ Day](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Disney%2B_Day "Disney+ Day")" celebration.[[429]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-Disney+DaySpecial-433)[[430]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-Disney+Day-434)

### Documentary series

#### _Marvel Studios: Legends_ (2021–present)

Main article: [_Marvel Studios: Legends_](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Studios:_Legends "Marvel Studios: Legends")

Announced in December 2020, this series examines individual heroes, villains, moments, and objects from the Marvel Cinematic Universe and how they connect, in anticipation of the upcoming stories that will feature them in Phase Four.[[431]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-Legends-435)[[432]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-LokiLegends-436)_Marvel Studios: Legends_ premiered on Disney+ on January 8, 2021, with the release of the first two episodes.[[431]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-Legends-435) Additional episodes were released ahead of a character and objects' appearances in Disney+ series and films.[[431]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-Legends-435)[[433]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-BWLegendsLokiAssembled-437)

#### _Marvel Studios: Assembled_ (2021–present)

Main article: [_Marvel Studios: Assembled_](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Studios:_Assembled "Marvel Studios: Assembled")

Announced in February 2021, each special of the documentary series goes behind the scenes of the making of the MCU films and television series with cast members and additional creatives. _Marvel Studios: Assembled_ premiered on Disney+ on March 12, 2021, with the release of the first special, followed by additional specials.[[434]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-Assembled-438)

#### _Voices Rising: The Music of Wakanda Forever_ (2023)

Further information: [_Black Panther: Wakanda Forever_ § Music](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Black_Panther:_Wakanda_Forever#Music "Black Panther: Wakanda Forever")

_Voices Rising: The Music of Wakanda Forever_ is a three-part documentary series detailing the creation process of _Black Panther: Wakanda Forever_'s soundtrack. It premiered on Disney+ on February 28, 2023.[[435]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-VoicesRisingMarvel-439) The documentary series was originally scheduled to be removed from Disney+ on May 26, 2023, as part of Disney's efforts to reduce content costs, but ultimately was decided to remain on the service at that time.[[436]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-DocsPlannedD+Removal-440)

#### _MPower_ (2023)

In June 2021, Marvel Studios released a casting call for fans of "Marvel's strong women" to be a part of an unscripted Disney+ documentary series showcasing the women who create the MCU in front of and behind the camera, including actors and creatives, and the fans who applied to participate in the series.[[437]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-SuperWomenCasting-441) The series was titled _MPower_ by February 2023 and premiered in its entirety on March 8, 2023,[[438]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPower-442) consisting of four episodes titled "The Women of Black Panther", "Captain Marvel", "Scarlet Witch", and "Gamora",[[439]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPowerComicBookDetails-443) which were directed by Quinn Wilson and used [archival footage](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Archival_footage "Archival footage") and animation.[[439]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPowerComicBookDetails-443)[[440]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPowerMarvelDetails-444) Its release coincided with [International Women's Day](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Women%27s_Day "International Women's Day").[[441]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPowerSRBWInsult-445) Several MCU actresses were interviewed to discuss what makes their characters compelling to audiences, including [Danai Gurira](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danai_Gurira "Danai Gurira"), [Lupita Nyong'o](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lupita_Nyong%27o "Lupita Nyong'o"), [Florence Kasumba](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Florence_Kasumba "Florence Kasumba"), and Letitia Wright; Brie Larson, Iman Vellani, and [Teyonah Parris](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Teyonah_Parris "Teyonah Parris"); [Elizabeth Olsen](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elizabeth_Olsen "Elizabeth Olsen"), [Kathryn Hahn](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kathryn_Hahn "Kathryn Hahn"), and [Kat Dennings](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kat_Dennings "Kat Dennings"); and Zoë Saldaña,[[439]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPowerComicBookDetails-443) who executive produced the series alongside Victoria Alonso. Saldaña said the series was a tribute to the representation and empowerment of women with the intent to "ignite meaningful conversations and drive real change towards a more equal and inclusive world."[[439]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPowerComicBookDetails-443)[[442]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPowerMarvelInterview-446)[[440]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPowerMarvelDetails-444) Other creatives who were interviewed for episodes include Marvel Studios executive [Trinh Tran](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Trinh_Tran "Trinh Tran"), _Black Panther_ costume designer [Ruth E. Carter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ruth_E._Carter "Ruth E. Carter"), production designer [Hannah Beachler](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hannah_Beachler "Hannah Beachler"), and editor [Debbie Berman](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Debbie_Berman "Debbie Berman").[[443]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPower/FilmDetails-447) The documentary series was originally scheduled to be removed from Disney+ on May 26, 2023, as part of Disney's efforts to reduce content costs, but ultimately was decided to remain on the service at that time.[[436]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-DocsPlannedD+Removal-440) The series was produced by [Herzog & Co.](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Herzog_%26_Co. "Herzog & Co."), Saldaña's production company [Cinestar Pictures](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cinestar_Pictures "Cinestar Pictures"), and [Just Entertainment](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Just_Entertainment "Just Entertainment").[[440]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPowerMarvelDetails-444)[[442]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPowerMarvelInterview-446)

Aaron Perine at _[ComicBook.com](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ComicBook.com "ComicBook.com")_ believed that the series would have "something for all fans to enjoy" with each character's entry because of the fan appreciation,[[439]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPowerComicBookDetails-443) while BJ Conagelo of _[/Film](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki//Film "/Film")_ stated it was "fantastic to see a thoughtful and in-depth spotlight" of the work by diverse groups of women in the MCU, and found it was "equally as impressive" how much the series analyzed their impact as a "sincere assessment" of the importance of the stories beyond [gender representation](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gender_representation "Gender representation").[[443]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPower/FilmDetails-447) Philip Watson at _CGMagazine_ said that while the series seemed focused on "add[ing] depth" to the backstories of the females behind Marvel, a secondary focus was to honor the title and empower women, quoting Kasumba: "You could watch it and think 'people that look like me, we can be Super Heroes too'".[[444]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPowerCGMagazineDetails-448) Kai Young of _Screen Rant_ felt that the series' exclusion of an episode focused on [Scarlett Johansson](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scarlett_Johansson "Scarlett Johansson")'s MCU character Natasha Romanoff / Black Widow was another "insult against" the character as she was "pivotal to the MCU", and had wanted such an episode to focus on developing Romanoff as an individual beyond her relationships with male characters and alongside her family.[[441]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MPowerSRBWInsult-445)

### Literary material

In September 2015, Marvel announced the _Guidebook to the Marvel Cinematic Universe_, named as a nod to the _[Official Handbook of the Marvel Universe](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Official\_Handbook\_of\_the\_Marvel\_Universe "Official Handbook of the Marvel Universe")_. Each guidebook is compiled by Mike O'Sullivan and the _Official Handbook of the Marvel Universe_ team, with cover art from [Mike del Mundo](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mike_del_Mundo "Mike del Mundo") and Pascal Campion, and features facts about the MCU films, film-to-comic comparisons, and production stills. The guidebooks released each month from October 2015 to January 2016 were _Guidebook to the Marvel Cinematic Universe: Marvel's Iron Man_, _Guidebook to the Marvel Cinematic Universe: Marvel's Incredible Hulk / Marvel's Iron Man 2_,[[445]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-Guidebook-449)_Guidebook to the Marvel Cinematic Universe: Marvel's Thor_,[[446]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-GuidebookThor-450) and _Guidebook to the Marvel Cinematic Universe: Marvel's Captain America: The First Avenger_.[[447]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-GuidebookCapTFA-451)

In November 2018, Marvel and [Titan Publishing Group](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Titan_Publishing_Group "Titan Publishing Group") released _Marvel Studios: The First Ten Years_ to celebrate the first ten years of the MCU. It features cast interviews, in-depth sections on each film, and an Easter egg guide.[[448]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-TitanFirstTenYears-452) In October 2021, a two-volume book _The Story of Marvel Studios: The Making of the Marvel Cinematic Universe_ was released, written by Tara Bennett and Paul Terry. This collection features a look at the evolution of Marvel Studios, personal stories from the 23-film "Infinity Saga", and interviews with cast and crew members.[[449]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MakingOfMCU-453)

In April 2023, [W. W. Norton & Company](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/W._W._Norton_%26_Company "W. W. Norton & Company") announced _MCU: The Reign of Marvel Studios_ by Joanna Robinson, Dave Gonzales, and [Gavin Edwards](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gavin_Edwards_(writer) "Gavin Edwards (writer)"),[[450]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MCUReignOfMarvelStudios-454) for release on October 10, 2023.[[451]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MCUReign/Film-455) The book presents an unauthorized look at "the rise and uncertain reign of the MCU, analyzing Marvel Studios' place as a major player in Hollywood and global pop culture" from Marvel Studios' inception, through events in early 2023, conducted through numerous interviews with those closely associated with the MCU. Norton approached the writers in 2019 to work on a book centered on the MCU. Robinson explained that the book was originally meant to be an oral history, until Disney was no longer enthused about the book's publication despite initially being open to it, and told current employees and former stars not to talk to the writers. The writers were able to supplement the interviews they were able to get with those from "cultural critics and comics experts" in addition to years of research. Robinson added that because of the long work put into the book, it was able to cover the studio's expansion to television on Disney+, as well as "this current state of what I like to call a 'wobble' in Marvel's long reign", and provide "a lot of answers about how we got here". Additionally, the book was not deterred by the then-recent firings of Alonso and Marvel Entertainment CEO [Ike Perlmutter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ike_Perlmutter "Ike Perlmutter"), needing only "a few cosmetic tweaks to weave the whole story together" with Robinson explaining those firings "actually reinforced our sense that we really had captured the story of Marvel in both its triumphs and its stumbling blocks".[[450]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MCUReignOfMarvelStudios-454) Robinson was able to interview many of the subjects while Gonazles did the majority of the book's research, with Edwards compiling it all to give the book a "flow".[[451]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MCUReign/Film-455)

In February 2024, [Abrams Books](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abrams_Books "Abrams Books") announced _Marvel Studios: The Art of Ryan Meinerding_, written by Bennett and Terry. The book includes over 500 of Meinerding's illustrations, from work-in-progress to completed pieces, along with interview material in which Meinerding discusses his process and his work in Marvel Studios' visual development department. It was released on October 1, 2024.[[452]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MeinerdingBook-456)

### _A Mini Marvel_

In February 2016, a commercial for [Coca-Cola](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Coca-Cola "Coca-Cola") mini cans aired during [Super Bowl 50](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Super_Bowl_50 "Super Bowl 50"). _A Mini Marvel_ was created by [Wieden+Kennedy](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wieden%2BKennedy "Wieden+Kennedy") for Coca-Cola through a partnership with Marvel, and was directed by the Russo brothers.[[477]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-SuperBowl50Coke-481)[[478]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-SuperBowl50Coke2-482) In the ad, Ant-Man (voiced by Paul Rudd, reprising his role) and the Hulk first fight, and then bond, over a Coke mini can.[[477]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-SuperBowl50Coke-481)[Luma Pictures](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luma_Pictures "Luma Pictures") provided visual effects for the spot, having worked previously with the two characters in MCU films. For the Hulk, Luma redefined its previous muscular system and simulation process to create and render the character, while Ant-Man received new motion capture.[[478]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-SuperBowl50Coke2-482) The Super Bowl campaign extended to "limited-edition Coke mini cans [six packs] that are emblazoned with images of Marvel characters, including Hulk, Ant-Man, Black Widow, [Falcon, Iron Man] and Captain America." Consumers had the opportunity to purchase the cans by finding hidden clues in the commercial, though "if the program goes well, Coke will consider making the cans available in stores."[[477]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-SuperBowl50Coke-481) The ad had the third most social media activity of all the film-related trailers that aired during the game,[[479]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-DeadlineCoke-483) and was nominated for Outstanding Visual Effects in a Commercial at the [15th Visual Effects Society Awards](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Visual_Effects_Society_Awards_2016 "Visual Effects Society Awards 2016").[[480]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-MiniMarvelVESA-484)

### _The Good, the Bart, and the Loki_

Main article: [The Good, the Bart, and the Loki](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Good,_the_Bart,_and_the_Loki "The Good, the Bart, and the Loki")

In June 2021, _[The Simpsons](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The\_Simpsons "The Simpsons")_ short film _The Good, the Bart, and the Loki_ was announced, which was released alongside "[Journey into Mystery](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Journey_into_Mystery_(Loki) "Journey into Mystery (Loki)")", the fifth episode of _Loki_ on Disney+. The short sees Loki teaming up with [Bart Simpson](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bart_Simpson "Bart Simpson") in a crossover that pays homage to the heroes and villains of the MCU. Hiddleston reprises his role as Loki in the short.[[481]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marvel_Cinematic_Universe#cite_note-SimpsonsShort-485)
